                  <div _ngcontent-c19="" class="rich-text" innerhtml="<h3>Week of May 31-Jun 4 2021</h3><ul><li><b>Security Command Center now supports CIS 1.1 benchmarks and granular access control</b>&amp;#8211;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/security-command-center&quot;>Security Command Center</a> (SCC) now supports <a href=&quot;https://www.cisecurity.org/benchmark/google_cloud_computing_platform/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;>CIS benchmarks for Google Cloud Platform Foundation v1.1</a>, enabling you to monitor and address compliance violations against industry best practices in your Google Cloud environment. Additionally, SCC now supports fine-grained access control for administrators that allows you to easily adhere to the principles of least privilege&amp;#8212;restricting access based on roles and responsibilities to reduce risk and enabling broader team engagement to address security. <a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/new-capabilities-in-security-command-center-help-manage-risk&quot;>Read more</a>.<br></li><li><b>Zero-trust managed security for services with Traffic Director</b>&amp;#8211;We created <a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/traffic-director&quot;>Traffic Director</a> to bring to you a fully managed service mesh product that includes load balancing, traffic management and service discovery. And now, we&amp;#8217;re happy to announce the availability of a fully-managed zero-trust security solution using Traffic Director with Google Kubernetes Engine (GKE) and <a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/certificate-authority-service&quot;>Certificate Authority (CA) Service</a>. <a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/networking/traffic-director-integrates-with-ca-service&quot;>Read more</a>.</li><li><b>How one business modernized their data warehouse for customer success</b>&amp;#8211;PedidosYa migrated from their old data warehouse to Google Cloud's BigQuery. Now with BigQuery, the Latin American online food ordering company has reduced the total cost per query by 5x. <a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/data-analytics/pedidosya-cuts-cost-per-query-by-5x-using-bigquery&quot;>Learn more</a>.</li><li><b>Announcing new Cloud TPU VMs</b>&amp;#8211;New Cloud TPU VMs make it easier to use our <a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/ai-machine-learning/google-breaks-ai-performance-records-in-mlperf-with-worlds-fastest-training-supercomputer&quot;>industry-leading TPU hardware</a> by providing direct access to TPU host machines, offering a new and improved user experience to develop and deploy TensorFlow, PyTorch, and JAX on <a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/tpu&quot;>Cloud TPUs</a>. <a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/compute/introducing-cloud-tpu-vms&quot;>Read more</a>.<br></li><li><b>Introducing logical replication and decoding for Cloud SQL for PostgreSQL</b>&amp;#8211;We&amp;#8217;re announcing the public preview of <a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/sql/docs/postgres/replication/configure-logical-replication&quot;>logical replication and decoding for Cloud SQL for PostgreSQL.</a> By releasing those capabilities and enabling change data capture (CDC) from Cloud SQL for PostgreSQL, we strengthen our commitment to building an open database platform that meets critical application requirements and integrates seamlessly with <a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/sql/docs/postgres&quot;>the PostgreSQL ecosystem</a>. <a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/databases/you-can-now-use-cdc-from-cloudsql-for-postgresql&quot;>Read more</a>.<br></li><li><b>How 6 businesses are transforming with SAP on Google Cloud</b>&amp;#8211;Thousands of organizations globally rely on SAP for their most mission critical workloads. And for many Google Cloud customers, part of a broader digital transformation journey has included accelerating the migration of these essential SAP workloads to Google Cloud for greater agility, elasticity, and uptime. <a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/sap-google-cloud/6-businesses-transforming-sap-google-cloud&quot;>Read six of their stories</a>.</li></ul>">
                   <h3>Week of May 31-Jun 4 2021</h3>
                   <ul>
                    <li><b>Security Command Center now supports CIS 1.1 benchmarks and granular access control</b><a href="https://cloud.google.com/security-command-center" track-type="inline link" track-name="3" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/security-command-center" track-metadata-module="post">Security Command Center</a> (SCC) now supports <a href="https://www.cisecurity.org/benchmark/google_cloud_computing_platform/" target="_blank" track-type="inline link" track-name="4" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://www.cisecurity.org" track-metadata-module="post">CIS benchmarks for Google Cloud Platform Foundation v1.1</a>, enabling you to monitor and address compliance violations against industry best practices in your Google Cloud environment. Additionally, SCC now supports fine-grained access control for administrators that allows you to easily adhere to the principles of least privilegerestricting access based on roles and responsibilities to reduce risk and enabling broader team engagement to address security. <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/new-capabilities-in-security-command-center-help-manage-risk" track-type="inline link" track-name="5" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/new-capabilities-in-security-command-center-help-manage-risk" track-metadata-module="post">Read more</a>.<br></li>
                    <li><b>Zero-trust managed security for services with Traffic Director</b>We created <a href="https://cloud.google.com/traffic-director" track-type="inline link" track-name="6" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/traffic-director" track-metadata-module="post">Traffic Director</a> to bring to you a fully managed service mesh product that includes load balancing, traffic management and service discovery. And now, were happy to announce the availability of a fully-managed zero-trust security solution using Traffic Director with Google Kubernetes Engine (GKE) and <a href="https://cloud.google.com/certificate-authority-service" track-type="inline link" track-name="7" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/certificate-authority-service" track-metadata-module="post">Certificate Authority (CA) Service</a>. <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/networking/traffic-director-integrates-with-ca-service" track-type="inline link" track-name="8" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/networking/traffic-director-integrates-with-ca-service" track-metadata-module="post">Read more</a>.</li>
                    <li><b>How one business modernized their data warehouse for customer success</b>PedidosYa migrated from their old data warehouse to Google Cloud's BigQuery. Now with BigQuery, the Latin American online food ordering company has reduced the total cost per query by 5x. <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/data-analytics/pedidosya-cuts-cost-per-query-by-5x-using-bigquery" track-type="inline link" track-name="9" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/data-analytics/pedidosya-cuts-cost-per-query-by-5x-using-bigquery" track-metadata-module="post">Learn more</a>.</li>
                    <li><b>Announcing new Cloud TPU VMs</b>New Cloud TPU VMs make it easier to use our <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/ai-machine-learning/google-breaks-ai-performance-records-in-mlperf-with-worlds-fastest-training-supercomputer" track-type="inline link" track-name="10" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/ai-machine-learning/google-breaks-ai-performance-records-in-mlperf-with-worlds-fastest-training-supercomputer" track-metadata-module="post">industry-leading TPU hardware</a> by providing direct access to TPU host machines, offering a new and improved user experience to develop and deploy TensorFlow, PyTorch, and JAX on <a href="https://cloud.google.com/tpu" track-type="inline link" track-name="11" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/tpu" track-metadata-module="post">Cloud TPUs</a>. <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/compute/introducing-cloud-tpu-vms" track-type="inline link" track-name="12" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/compute/introducing-cloud-tpu-vms" track-metadata-module="post">Read more</a>.<br></li>
                    <li><b>Introducing logical replication and decoding for Cloud SQL for PostgreSQL</b>Were announcing the public preview of <a href="https://cloud.google.com/sql/docs/postgres/replication/configure-logical-replication" track-type="inline link" track-name="13" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/sql/docs/postgres/replication/configure-logical-replication" track-metadata-module="post">logical replication and decoding for Cloud SQL for PostgreSQL.</a> By releasing those capabilities and enabling change data capture (CDC) from Cloud SQL for PostgreSQL, we strengthen our commitment to building an open database platform that meets critical application requirements and integrates seamlessly with <a href="https://cloud.google.com/sql/docs/postgres" track-type="inline link" track-name="14" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/sql/docs/postgres" track-metadata-module="post">the PostgreSQL ecosystem</a>. <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/databases/you-can-now-use-cdc-from-cloudsql-for-postgresql" track-type="inline link" track-name="15" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/databases/you-can-now-use-cdc-from-cloudsql-for-postgresql" track-metadata-module="post">Read more</a>.<br></li>
                    <li><b>How 6 businesses are transforming with SAP on Google Cloud</b>Thousands of organizations globally rely on SAP for their most mission critical workloads. And for many Google Cloud customers, part of a broader digital transformation journey has included accelerating the migration of these essential SAP workloads to Google Cloud for greater agility, elasticity, and uptime. <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/sap-google-cloud/6-businesses-transforming-sap-google-cloud" track-type="inline link" track-name="16" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/sap-google-cloud/6-businesses-transforming-sap-google-cloud" track-metadata-module="post">Read six of their stories</a>.</li>
                   </ul>

                  <div _ngcontent-c19="" class="rich-text" innerhtml="<h3>Week of May 17-May 21 2021</h3><ul><li><p><b>Best practices to protect your organization against ransomware threats</b>&amp;#8211;For more than 20 years Google has been operating securely in the cloud, using our modern technology stack to provide a more defensible environment that we can protect at scale. While the threat of ransomware isn&amp;#8217;t new, our responsibility to help protect you from existing or emerging threats never changes.                    <h3>Week of May 17-May 21 2021</h3>

                    <li><p><b>Best practices to protect your organization against ransomware threats</b>For more than 20 years Google has been operating securely in the cloud, using our modern technology stack to provide a more defensible environment that we can protect at scale.                     <li><b>Forrester names Google Cloud a Leader in Unstructured Data Security Platforms</b>Forrester Research has named Google Cloud a Leader in The Forrester Wave: Unstructured Data Security Platforms, Q2 2021 report, and rated Google Cloud highest in the current offering category among the providers evaluated. <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/google-a-leader-in-unstructured-data-security-platforms" track-type="inline link" track-name="43" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/google-a-leader-in-unstructured-data-security-platforms" track-metadata-module="post">Read more</a>&nbsp;or <a href="https://cloud.google.com/resources/forrester-unstructured-data-security-2021-report" track-type="inline link" track-name="44" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/resources/forrester-unstructured-data-security-2021-report" track-metadata-module="post">download the report</a>.<br></li>
                    <li><b>Introducing Vertex AI: One platform, every ML tool you need</b><a href="https://cloud.google.com/vertex-ai" track-type="inline link" track-name="45" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/vertex-ai" track-metadata-module="post">Vertex AI</a>&nbsp;is a managed machine learning (ML) platform that allows companies to accelerate the deployment and maintenance of artificial intelligence (AI) models. <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/ai-machine-learning/google-cloud-launches-vertex-ai-unified-platform-for-mlops" track-type="inline link" track-name="46" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/ai-machine-learning/google-cloud-launches-vertex-ai-unified-platform-for-mlops" track-metadata-module="post">Read more</a>.</li>
                    <li><b>Transforming collaboration in Google Workspace</b>Were launching&nbsp;smart canvas,&nbsp;a new product experience that delivers the next evolution of collaboration for Google Workspace.                     <li><b>Contributing to an environment of trust and transparency in Europe</b>Google Cloud was one of the first cloud providers to support and adopt the&nbsp;<a href="https://scope-europe.eu/en/projects/eu-cloud-code-of-conduct/" target="_blank" track-type="inline link" track-name="49" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://scope-europe.eu" track-metadata-module="post">EU GDPR Cloud Code of Conduct&nbsp;</a>(CoC). These same tools protect customers&amp;#8217; infrastructure from DDoS attacks, which are increasing in both magnitude and complexity every year. Deployed at the very edge of our network, Cloud Armor absorbs malicious network- and protocol-based volumetric attacks, while mitigating the <a href=&quot;https://owasp.org/www-project-top-ten/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;>OWASP Top 10 risks</a> and maintaining the availability of protected services. <a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/google-cloud-armor-managed-protection-plus-is-now-ga&quot;>Read more</a>.<br></li><li><b>Announcing Document Translation for Translation API Advanced in preview</b>&amp;#8211;Translation is critical to many developers and localization providers, whether you&amp;#8217;re releasing a document, a piece of software, training materials or a website in multiple languages. With Document Translation, now you can directly translate documents in 100+ languages and formats such as Docx, PPTx, XLSx, and PDF while preserving document formatting. <a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/ai-machine-learning/google-cloud-ai-translation-services-works-for-documents&quot;>Read more</a>.<br></li><li><b>Introducing BeyondCorp Enterprise protected profiles</b>&amp;#8211;Protected profiles enable users to securely access corporate resources from an unmanaged device with the same threat and data protections available in BeyondCorp Enterprise&amp;#8211;all from the Chrome Browser. <a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/new-protected-profiles-enable-remote-work-with-zero-trust&quot;>Read more</a>.<br></li><li><b>How reCAPTCHA Enterprise protects unemployment and COVID-19 vaccination portals</b>&amp;#8211;With so many people visiting government websites to learn more about the COVID-19 vaccine, make vaccine appointments, or file for unemployment, these web pages have become prime targets for bot attacks and other abusive activities. But reCAPTCHA Enterprise has helped state governments protect COVID-19 vaccine registration portals and unemployment claims portals from abusive activities. <a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/recaptcha-protects-public-services&quot;>Learn more</a>.</li><li><b>Day one with Anthos? Here are 6 ideas for how to get started</b>&amp;#8211;Once you have your new application platform in place, there are some things you can do to immediately get value and gain momentum. Here are six things you can do to get you started. <a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/anthos/6-initiatives-to-start-on-your-day-one-anthos-journey&quot;>Read more</a>.</li><li><b>The era of the transformation cloud is here</b>&amp;#8211;Google Cloud&amp;#8217;s president Rob Enslin shares how the era of the transformation cloud has seen organizations move beyond data centers to change not only where their business is done but, more importantly, how it is done. <a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/inside-google-cloud/innovation-in-the-era-of-the-transformation-cloud&quot;>Read more</a>.</li></ul>">
                   <h3>Week of May 10-May 14 2021</h3>
                   <ul>
                    <li><b>APIs and Apigee power modern day due diligence</b>With APIs and Google Cloud's Apigee, business due diligence company DueDil revolutionized the way they harness and share their Big Information Graph (B.I.G.) with partners and customers. <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/apigee/google-cloud-helps-duedil-to-deliver-data-insights-at-scale" track-type="inline link" track-name="65" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/apigee/google-cloud-helps-duedil-to-deliver-data-insights-at-scale" track-metadata-module="post">Get the full story</a>.<br></li>
                    <li><b>Cloud CISO Perspectives: May 2021</b>Its been a busy month here at Google Cloud since our inaugural CISO perspectives blog post in April. Here, VP and CISO of Google Cloud Phil Venables recaps our cloud security and industry highlights, a sneak peak of whats ahead from Google at RSA, and more. <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/cloud-ciso-perspectives-may-2021" track-type="inline link" track-name="66" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/cloud-ciso-perspectives-may-2021" track-metadata-module="post">Read more</a>.</li>
                    <li><b>4 new features to secure your Cloud Run services</b>We announced several new ways to secure Cloud Run environments to make developing and deploying containerized applications easier for developers. <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/serverless/improving-the-security-of-your-cloud-run-environment" track-type="inline link" track-name="67" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/serverless/improving-the-security-of-your-cloud-run-environment" track-metadata-module="post">Read more</a>.</li>
                    <li><b>Maximize your Cloud Run investments with new committed use discounts</b>Were introducing self-service spend-based <a href="https://cloud.google.com/run/cud" track-type="inline link" track-name="68" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/run/cud" track-metadata-module="post">committed use discounts for Cloud Run</a>, which let you commit for a year to spending a certain amount on Cloud Run and benefiting from a 17% discount on the amount you committed. <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/serverless/introducing-committed-use-discounts-for-cloud-run" track-type="inline link" track-name="69" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/serverless/introducing-committed-use-discounts-for-cloud-run" track-metadata-module="post">Read more</a>.</li>
                    <li><b>Google Cloud Armor Managed Protection Plus is now generally available</b>Cloud Armor, our Distributed Denial of Service (DDoS) protection and Web-Application Firewall (WAF) service on Google Cloud, leverages the same infrastructure, network, and technology that has protected Googles internet-facing properties from some of the <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/identifying-and-protecting-against-the-largest-ddos-attacks" track-type="inline link" track-name="70" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/identifying-and-protecting-against-the-largest-ddos-attacks" track-metadata-module="post">largest attacks ever reported</a>. These same tools protect customers infrastructure from DDoS attacks, which are increasing in both magnitude and complexity every year. Deployed at the very edge of our network, Cloud Armor absorbs malicious network- and protocol-based volumetric attacks, while mitigating the <a href="https://owasp.org/www-project-top-ten/" target="_blank" track-type="inline link" track-name="71" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://owasp.org" track-metadata-module="post">OWASP Top 10 risks</a> and maintaining the availability of protected services. <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/google-cloud-armor-managed-protection-plus-is-now-ga" track-type="inline link" track-name="72" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/google-cloud-armor-managed-protection-plus-is-now-ga" track-metadata-module="post">Read more</a>.<br></li>
                    <li><b>Announcing Document Translation for Translation API Advanced in preview</b>Translation is critical to many developers and localization providers, whether youre releasing a document, a piece of software, training materials or a website in multiple languages. With Document Translation, now you can directly translate documents in 100+ languages and formats such as Docx, PPTx, XLSx, and PDF while preserving document formatting. <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/ai-machine-learning/google-cloud-ai-translation-services-works-for-documents" track-type="inline link" track-name="73" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/ai-machine-learning/google-cloud-ai-translation-services-works-for-documents" track-metadata-module="post">Read more</a>.<br></li>
                    <li><b>Introducing BeyondCorp Enterprise protected profiles</b>Protected profiles enable users to securely access corporate resources from an unmanaged device with the same threat and data protections available in BeyondCorp Enterpriseall from the Chrome Browser. <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/new-protected-profiles-enable-remote-work-with-zero-trust" track-type="inline link" track-name="74" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/new-protected-profiles-enable-remote-work-with-zero-trust" track-metadata-module="post">Read more</a>.<br></li>
                    <li><b>How reCAPTCHA Enterprise protects unemployment and COVID-19 vaccination portals</b>With so many people visiting government websites to learn more about the COVID-19 vaccine, make vaccine appointments, or file for unemployment, these web pages have become prime targets for bot attacks and other abusive activities. But reCAPTCHA Enterprise has helped state governments protect COVID-19 vaccine registration portals and unemployment claims portals from abusive activities. <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/recaptcha-protects-public-services" track-type="inline link" track-name="75" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/recaptcha-protects-public-services" track-metadata-module="post">Learn more</a>.</li>
                    <li><b>Day one with Anthos? Here are 6 ideas for how to get started</b>Once you have your new application platform in place, there are some things you can do to immediately get value and gain momentum. Here are six things you can do to get you started. <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/anthos/6-initiatives-to-start-on-your-day-one-anthos-journey" track-type="inline link" track-name="76" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/anthos/6-initiatives-to-start-on-your-day-one-anthos-journey" track-metadata-module="post">Read more</a>.</li>
                    <li><b>The era of the transformation cloud is here</b>Google Clouds president Rob Enslin shares how the era of the transformation cloud has seen organizations move beyond data centers to change not only where their business is done but, more importantly, how it is done. <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/inside-google-cloud/innovation-in-the-era-of-the-transformation-cloud" track-type="inline link" track-name="77" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/inside-google-cloud/innovation-in-the-era-of-the-transformation-cloud" track-metadata-module="post">Read more</a>.</li>
                   </ul>

                    <li><b>Cloud computing 101: Frequently asked questions</b>There are a number of terms and concepts in cloud computing, and not everyone is familiar with all of them. It allows users to do informed planning of their deployment architecture, as well as determine in real time the answer to the most common troubleshooting question: &amp;#34;Is it Google or is it me?&amp;#34; The Google Cloud performance view is now open for all Google Cloud customers as a public preview.&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://console.cloud.google.com/net-intelligence/performance/global-dashboard/packet-loss&quot;>Check it out</a>.</li><li><b>Optimizing data in Google Sheets allows users to create no-code apps</b>&amp;#8211;Format columns and tables in Google Sheets to best position your data to transform into a fully customized, successful app&amp;#8211;no coding necessary. However, declaring a configuration is only half the battle: you also want policy that defines how a configuration is to be used. <a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/containers-kubernetes/how-configuration-as-data-impacts-policy&quot;>This post shows you how</a>.<br></li><li><b>Google Cloud products deliver real-time data solutions</b>&amp;#8211;Seven-Eleven Japan built Seven Central, its new platform for digital transformation, on Google Cloud. Powered by BigQuery, Cloud Spanner, and Apigee API management, Seven Central presents easy to understand data, ultimately allowing for quickly informed decisions. Read their story <a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/data-analytics/how-7-eleven-japan-built-its-new-data-platform&quot;>here</a>.</li></ul>">

It allows users to do informed planning of their deployment architecture, as well as determine in real time the answer to the most common troubleshooting question: "Is it Google or is it me?"                    <h3>Week of Apr 19-Apr 23 2021</h3>
                   <p></p>
                   <p></p>
                   <ul>
                    <li><p><b>Extreme PD is now GA</b>On April 20th, Google Clouds <a href="https://cloud.google.com/persistent-disk" track-type="inline link" track-name="117" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/persistent-disk" track-metadata-module="post">Persistent Disk</a> launched general availability of Extreme PD, a high performance block storage volume with provisioned IOPS and up to 2.2 GB/s of throughput.&nbsp;<a href="https://cloud.google.com/compute/docs/disks/extreme-persistent-disk" track-type="inline link" track-name="118" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/compute/docs/disks/extreme-persistent-disk" track-metadata-module="post">Learn more</a>.<br></p></li>
                    <li><p><b>Research: How data analytics and intelligence tools to play a key role post-COVID-19</b>A recent&nbsp;<a href="https://inthecloud.withgoogle.com/it-leaders-research-21/overview-dl-cd.html?utm_source=google&amp;utm_medium=blog&amp;utm_campaign=FY21-Q1-NORTHAM-demandgen-website-wd-gcp_gtm_reimagine_master&amp;utm_content=homepage" target="_blank" track-type="inline link" track-name="119" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://inthecloud.withgoogle.com" track-metadata-module="post">Google-commissioned study by IDG</a>&nbsp;highlighted the role of data analytics and intelligent solutions when it comes to helping businesses separate from their competition. The survey of 2,000 IT leaders across the globe reinforced the notion that the ability to derive insights from data will go a long way towards determining which companies win in this new era.&nbsp;<a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/data-analytics/post-covid-data-analytics-and-intelligence-tools" track-type="inline link" track-name="120" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/data-analytics/post-covid-data-analytics-and-intelligence-tools" track-metadata-module="post">Learn more</a>&nbsp;or&nbsp;<a href="https://inthecloud.withgoogle.com/it-leaders-research-21/overview-dl-cd.html?utm_source=google&amp;utm_medium=blog&amp;utm_campaign=FY21-Q1-NORTHAM-demandgen-website-wd-gcp_gtm_reimagine_master&amp;utm_content=homepage" target="_blank" track-type="inline link" track-name="121" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://inthecloud.withgoogle.com" track-metadata-module="post">download the study</a>.</p></li>
                    <li><p><b>Introducing PHP on Cloud Functions</b>Were bringing support for PHP, a popular general-purpose programming language, to Cloud Functions. With the Functions Framework for PHP, you can write idiomatic PHP functions to build business-critical applications and integration layers. And with Cloud Functions for PHP, now available in Preview, you can deploy functions in a fully managed PHP 7.4 environment, complete with access to resources in a private VPC network.&nbsp;<a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/application-development/php-comes-to-cloud-functions" track-type="inline link" track-name="122" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/application-development/php-comes-to-cloud-functions" track-metadata-module="post">Learn more</a>.</p></li>

        h-c-grid__col--offset-2 h-c-grid__col-m--offset-3 h-c-grid__col-l--offset-3 uni-click-tracker" clicktracker="" track-metadata-module="related article tout" track-type="article" track-name="SRE fundamentals 2021: SLIs vs SLAs vs SLOs" track-metadata-eventdetail="/products/devops-sre/sre-fundamentals-sli-vs-slo-vs-sla/" href="/blog/products/devops-sre/sre-fundamentals-sli-vs-slo-vs-sla">

                    <div class="uni-related-article-tout__image-wrapper ng-star-inserted">
                     <div class="uni-related-article-tout__image" style="background-image:url(https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/DevOps_BlogHeader_B_Rnd3.max-600x600.jpg);"></div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="uni-related-article-tout__content">
                     <h4 class="uni-related-article-tout__header h-has-bottom-margin">SRE fundamentals 2021: SLIs vs SLAs vs SLOs</h4>
                     <p class="uni-related-article-tout__body">Whats the difference between an SLI, an SLO and an SLA? Google Site Reliability Engineers (SRE) explain.</p>
                     <div class="cta module-cta h-c-copy  uni-related-article-tout__cta muted">
                      <span class="nowrap">Read Article</span>
                      <svg class="icon h-c-icon" role="presentation">
                       <use xlink:href="#mi-arrow-forward" xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink"></use>
                      </svg>

              <div class="module--text h-c-page ng-star-inserted">
               <div class="h-c-grid">
                <div class="uni-paragraph
          h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--8 h-c-grid__col-m--6 h-c-grid__col-l--6
          h-c-grid__col--offset-2 h-c-grid__col-m--offset-3 h-c-grid__col-l--offset-3">
                 <!----><!----><paragraph-block _nghost-c19="" class="ng-star-inserted">
                  <div _ngcontent-c19="" class="rich-text" innerhtml="<h3>Week of Apr 5-Apr 9 2021<br></h3><p></p><ul><li><b>New Certificate Authority Service (CAS) whitepaper</b>&amp;#8211;&amp;#8220;How to deploy a secure and reliable public key infrastructure with Google Cloud Certificate Authority Service&amp;#8221; (written by Mark Cooper of PKI Solutions and Anoosh Saboori of Google Cloud) covers security and architectural recommendations for the use of the Google Cloud CAS by organizations, and describes critical concepts for securing and deploying a PKI based on CAS.&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/how-to-deploy-google-cas-whitepaper&quot;>Learn more</a>&amp;#160;or read the&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://services.google.com/fh/files/misc/deploying_public_key_infrastructure_with_cas.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;>whitepaper</a>.<br></li><li><b>Active Assist&amp;#8217;s new feature,&amp;#160;<i>predictive autoscaling</i>, helps improve response times for your applications</b>&amp;#8211;When you enable predictive autoscaling, Compute Engine forecasts future load based on your Managed Instance Group&amp;#8217;s (MIG) history and scales it out in advance of predicted load, so that new instances are ready to serve when the load arrives. Without predictive autoscaling, an autoscaler can only scale a group reactively, based on observed changes in load in real time. With predictive autoscaling enabled, the autoscaler works with real-time data as well as with historical data to cover both the current and forecasted load. That makes predictive autoscaling ideal for those apps with long initialization times and whose workloads vary predictably with daily or weekly cycles. For more information, see&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/compute/docs/autoscaler/predictive-autoscaling#how_predictive_autoscaling_works&quot;>How predictive autoscaling works</a>&amp;#160;or&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/compute/docs/autoscaler/predictive-autoscaling#checking_if_predictive_autoscaling_is_suitable_for_your_workload&quot;>check if predictive autoscaling is suitable for your workload</a>, and to learn more about other intelligent features, check out&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/solutions/active-assist&quot;>Active Assist</a>.<br></li><li><b>Introducing Dataprep BigQuery pushdown</b>&amp;#8211;BigQuery pushdown gives you the flexibility to run jobs using either BigQuery or Dataflow. If you select BigQuery, then Dataprep can automatically determine if data pipelines can be partially or fully translated in a BigQuery SQL statement. Any portions of the pipeline that cannot be run in BigQuery are executed in Dataflow. Utilizing the power of BigQuery results in highly efficient data transformations, especially for manipulations such as filters, joins, unions, and aggregations. This leads to better performance, optimized costs, and increased security with IAM and OAuth support.&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/data-analytics/introducing-dataprep-bigquery-pushdown&quot;>Learn more</a>.<br></li><li><b>Announcing the Google Cloud Retail &amp;amp; Consumer Goods Summit</b>&amp;#8211;The Google Cloud Retail &amp;amp; Consumer Goods Summit brings together technology and business insights, the key ingredients for any transformation. Whether you're responsible for IT, data analytics, supply chains, or marketing, please join! Building connections and sharing perspectives cross-functionally is important to reimagining yourself, your organization, or the world.&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/events/google-cloud-retail-consumer-goods-summit-future-retail&quot;>Learn more</a>&amp;#160;or&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloudonair.withgoogle.com/events/retailsummit?utm_content=globalblog&amp;amp;utm_source=Google&amp;amp;utm_medium=blog&amp;amp;utm_campaign=FY21-Q2-emea-eventindustry-onlineevent-er-RetailHorizonSummit&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;>register for free</a>.</li><li><b>New IDC whitepaper assesses multicloud as a risk mitigation strategy</b>&amp;#8211;To better understand the benefits and challenges associated with a multicloud approach, we supported IDC&amp;#8217;s new whitepaper that investigates how multicloud can help regulated organizations mitigate the risks of using a single cloud vendor. The whitepaper looks at different approaches to multi-vendor and hybrid clouds taken by European organizations and how these strategies can help organizations address concentration risk and vendor-lock in, improve their compliance posture, and demonstrate an exit strategy.&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/hybrid-cloud/idc-whitepaper-assesses-multicloud-as-risk-mitigation-strategy&quot;>Learn more</a>&amp;#160;or&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://services.google.com/fh/files/misc/idc_multicloud_whitepaper.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;>download the paper</a>.</li><li><b>Introducing request priorities for Cloud Spanner APIs</b>&amp;#8211;You can now specify request priorities for some Cloud Spanner APIs. By assigning a HIGH, MEDIUM, or LOW priority to a specific request, you can now convey the relative importance of workloads, to better align resource usage with performance objectives.&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/developers-practitioners/introducing-request-priorities-cloud-spanner-apis&quot;>Learn more</a>.</li><li><b>How we&amp;#8217;re working with governments on climate goals</b>&amp;#8211;Google Sustainability Officer Kate Brandt shares more on how we&amp;#8217;re partnering with governments around the world to provide our technology and insights to drive progress in sustainability efforts.&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/public-sector/working-with-governments-on-climate-goals&quot;>Learn more</a>.</li></ul>">
                   <h3>Week of Apr 5-Apr 9 2021<br></h3>
                   <p></p>
                   <ul>
                    <li><b>New Certificate Authority Service (CAS) whitepaper</b>How to deploy a secure and reliable public key infrastructure with Google Cloud Certificate Authority Service (written by Mark Cooper of PKI Solutions and Anoosh Saboori of Google Cloud) covers security and architectural recommendations for the use of the Google Cloud CAS by organizations, and describes critical concepts for securing and deploying a PKI based on CAS.&nbsp;<a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/how-to-deploy-google-cas-whitepaper" track-type="inline link" track-name="149" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/how-to-deploy-google-cas-whitepaper" track-metadata-module="post">Learn more</a>&nbsp;or read the&nbsp;<a href="https://services.google.com/fh/files/misc/deploying_public_key_infrastructure_with_cas.pdf" target="_blank" track-type="inline link" track-name="150" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://services.google.com" track-metadata-module="post">whitepaper</a>.<br></li>
                    <li><b>Active Assists new feature,&nbsp;<i>predictive autoscaling</i>, helps improve response times for your applications</b>When you enable predictive autoscaling, Compute Engine forecasts future load based on your Managed Instance Groups (MIG) history and scales it out in advance of predicted load, so that new instances are ready to serve when the load arrives. Without predictive autoscaling, an autoscaler can only scale a group reactively, based on observed changes in load in real time. With predictive autoscaling enabled, the autoscaler works with real-time data as well as with historical data to cover both the current and forecasted load. That makes predictive autoscaling ideal for those apps with long initialization times and whose workloads vary predictably with daily or weekly cycles. For more information, see&nbsp;<a href="https://cloud.google.com/compute/docs/autoscaler/predictive-autoscaling#how_predictive_autoscaling_works" track-type="inline link" track-name="151" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/compute/docs/autoscaler/predictive-autoscaling#how_predictive_autoscaling_works" track-metadata-module="post">How predictive autoscaling works</a>&nbsp;or&nbsp;<a href="https://cloud.google.com/compute/docs/autoscaler/predictive-autoscaling#checking_if_predictive_autoscaling_is_suitable_for_your_workload" track-type="inline link" track-name="152" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/compute/docs/autoscaler/predictive-autoscaling#checking_if_predictive_autoscaling_is_suitable_for_your_workload" track-metadata-module="post">check if predictive autoscaling is suitable for your workload</a>, and to learn more about other intelligent features, check out&nbsp;<a href="https://cloud.google.com/solutions/active-assist" track-type="inline link" track-name="153" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/solutions/active-assist" track-metadata-module="post">Active Assist</a>.<br></li>
                    <li><b>Introducing Dataprep BigQuery pushdown</b>BigQuery pushdown gives you the flexibility to run jobs using either BigQuery or Dataflow. If you select BigQuery, then Dataprep can automatically determine if data pipelines can be partially or fully translated in a BigQuery SQL statement. Any portions of the pipeline that cannot be run in BigQuery are executed in Dataflow. Utilizing the power of BigQuery results in highly efficient data transformations, especially for manipulations such as filters, joins, unions, and aggregations. This leads to better performance, optimized costs, and increased security with IAM and OAuth support.&nbsp;<a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/data-analytics/introducing-dataprep-bigquery-pushdown" track-type="inline link" track-name="154" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/data-analytics/introducing-dataprep-bigquery-pushdown" track-metadata-module="post">Learn more</a>.<br></li>
                    <li><b>Announcing the Google Cloud Retail &amp; Consumer Goods Summit</b>The Google Cloud Retail &amp; Consumer Goods Summit brings together technology and business insights, the key ingredients for any transformation. Whether you're responsible for IT, data analytics, supply chains, or marketing, please join! Building connections and sharing perspectives cross-functionally is important to reimagining yourself, your organization, or the world.&nbsp;<a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/events/google-cloud-retail-consumer-goods-summit-future-retail" track-type="inline link" track-name="155" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/events/google-cloud-retail-consumer-goods-summit-future-retail" track-metadata-module="post">Learn more</a>&nbsp;or&nbsp;<a href="https://cloudonair.withgoogle.com/events/retailsummit?utm_content=globalblog&amp;utm_source=Google&amp;utm_medium=blog&amp;utm_campaign=FY21-Q2-emea-eventindustry-onlineevent-er-RetailHorizonSummit" target="_blank" track-type="inline link" track-name="156" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloudonair.withgoogle.com" track-metadata-module="post">register for free</a>.</li>
                    <li><b>New IDC whitepaper assesses multicloud as a risk mitigation strategy</b>To better understand the benefits and challenges associated with a multicloud approach, we supported IDCs new whitepaper that investigates how multicloud can help regulated organizations mitigate the risks of using a single cloud vendor. The whitepaper looks at different approaches to multi-vendor and hybrid clouds taken by European organizations and how these strategies can help organizations address concentration risk and vendor-lock in, improve their compliance posture, and demonstrate an exit strategy.&nbsp;<a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/hybrid-cloud/idc-whitepaper-assesses-multicloud-as-risk-mitigation-strategy" track-type="inline link" track-name="157" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/hybrid-cloud/idc-whitepaper-assesses-multicloud-as-risk-mitigation-strategy" track-metadata-module="post">Learn more</a>&nbsp;or&nbsp;<a href="https://services.google.com/fh/files/misc/idc_multicloud_whitepaper.pdf" target="_blank" track-type="inline link" track-name="158" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://services.google.com" track-metadata-module="post">download the paper</a>.</li>
                    <li><b>Introducing request priorities for Cloud Spanner APIs</b>You can now specify request priorities for some Cloud Spanner APIs. By assigning a HIGH, MEDIUM, or LOW priority to a specific request, you can now convey the relative importance of workloads, to better align resource usage with performance objectives.&nbsp;<a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/developers-practitioners/introducing-request-priorities-cloud-spanner-apis" track-type="inline link" track-name="159" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/developers-practitioners/introducing-request-priorities-cloud-spanner-apis" track-metadata-module="post">Learn more</a>.</li>
                    <li><b>How were working with governments on climate goals</b>Google Sustainability Officer Kate Brandt shares more on how were partnering with governments around the world to provide our technology and insights to drive progress in sustainability efforts.&nbsp;<a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/public-sector/working-with-governments-on-climate-goals" track-type="inline link" track-name="160" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/public-sector/working-with-governments-on-climate-goals" track-metadata-module="post">Learn more</a>.</li>
                   </ul>

Enterprises building and migrating open source data lakes to Google Cloud now have a central and persistent metastore for their open source data analytics frameworks.&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/data-analytics/data-lake-management-just-got-easier-dataproc-metastore-ga&quot;>Learn more</a>.</p></li><li><p><b>Introducing the Echo subsea cable</b>&amp;#8212;We announced our investment in Echo, the first-ever cable to directly connect the U.S. to Singapore with direct fiber pairs over an express route. This capability is a critical requirement to simplify identity management and streamline the migration of existing SQL Server workloads that rely on AD for access control.&nbsp;<a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/databases/windows-authentication-now-supported-by-googles-cloud-sql-database" track-type="inline link" track-name="170" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/databases/windows-authentication-now-supported-by-googles-cloud-sql-database" track-metadata-module="post">Learn more</a>&nbsp;or&nbsp;<a href="https://cloud.google.com/sql/docs/sqlserver/ad" track-type="inline link" track-name="171" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/sql/docs/sqlserver/ad" track-metadata-module="post">get started</a>.<br></p></li>
                    <li><p><b>Using Cloud AI to whip up new treats with Mars Maltesers</b>Maltesers, a popular British candy made by Mars, teamed up with our own&nbsp;<a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/developers-practitioners/baking-recipes-made-ai" track-type="inline link" track-name="172" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/developers-practitioners/baking-recipes-made-ai" track-metadata-module="post">AI baker</a>&nbsp;and ML engineer extraordinaire,&nbsp;<a href="https://twitter.com/SRobTweets" target="_blank" track-type="inline link" track-name="173" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://twitter.com" track-metadata-module="post">Sara Robinson</a>, to create a brand new dessert recipe with Google Cloud AI.&nbsp;<a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/ai-machine-learning/baking-with-maltesers-marmite-and-cloud-ai" track-type="inline link" track-name="174" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/ai-machine-learning/baking-with-maltesers-marmite-and-cloud-ai" track-metadata-module="post">Find out what happened</a>&nbsp;(recipe included).<br></p></li>
                    <li><p><b>Simplifying data lake management with Dataproc Metastore, now GA</b><a href="https://cloud.google.com/dataproc-metastore/docs" track-type="inline link" track-name="175" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/dataproc-metastore/docs" track-metadata-module="post">Dataproc Metastore</a>, a fully managed, serverless technical metadata repository based on the Apache Hive metastore, is now generally available. Enterprises building and migrating open source data lakes to Google Cloud now have a central and persistent metastore for their open source data analytics frameworks.&nbsp;<a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/data-analytics/data-lake-management-just-got-easier-dataproc-metastore-ga" track-type="inline link" track-name="176" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/data-analytics/data-lake-management-just-got-easier-dataproc-metastore-ga" track-metadata-module="post">Learn more</a>.</p></li>
                    <li><p><b>Introducing the Echo subsea cable</b>We announced our investment in Echo, the first-ever cable to directly connect the U.S. to Singapore with direct fiber pairs over an express route. Echo will run from Eureka, California to Singapore, with a stop-over in Guam, and plans to also land in Indonesia. Additional landings are possible in the future.&nbsp;<a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/infrastructure/introducing-the-echo-subsea-cable" track-type="inline link" track-name="177" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/infrastructure/introducing-the-echo-subsea-cable" track-metadata-module="post">Learn more</a>.</p></li>
                   </ul>
                  </div>
                 </paragraph-block><!----><!----><!---->

Network Connectivity Center serves as a vantage point to seamlessly connect VPNs, partner and dedicated interconnects, as well as third-party routers and Software-Defined WANs, helping you optimize connectivity, reduce operational burden and lower costs&amp;#8212;wherever your applications or users may be.&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/networking/announcing-network-connectivity-center&quot;>Learn more</a>.<br></li><li><b>Making it easier to get Compute Engine resources for batch processing</b>&amp;#8212;We announced a new method of obtaining&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/compute&quot;>Compute Engine</a>&amp;#160;instances for batch processing that accounts for availability of resources in zones of a region. Now available in preview for&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/compute/docs/instance-groups/regional-migs&quot;>regional managed instance groups</a>, you can do this simply by specifying the&amp;#160;<code>ANY</code>&amp;#160;value in the API.&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/hpc/a-new-way-to-obtain-compute-engine-vms-for-batch-processing&quot;>Learn more</a>.<br></li><li><b>Next-gen virtual automotive showrooms are here, thanks to Google Cloud, Unreal Engine, and NVIDIA</b>&amp;#8212;We teamed up with&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://www.unrealengine.com/en-US/industry/automotive-transportation&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;>Unreal Engine</a>, the open and advanced real-time 3D creation game engine, and NVIDIA, inventor of the GPU, to launch new virtual showroom experiences for automakers. Taking advantage of the&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://www.nvidia.com/en-us/design-visualization/solutions/rendering/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;>NVIDIA RTX platform</a>&amp;#160;on Google Cloud, these showrooms provide interactive 3D experiences, photorealistic materials and environments, and up to 4K cloud streaming on mobile and connected devices. Today, in collaboration with&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://www.mhp.com/en/company&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;>MHP</a>, the Porsche IT consulting firm, and&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://www.monkey-way.com/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;>MONKEYWAY</a>, a real-time 3D streaming solution provider, you can see our first virtual showroom, the Pagani Immersive Experience Platform.&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/retail/virtual-automotive-showrooms-with-google-cloud-unreal-engine-and-nvidia&quot;>Learn more</a>.<br></li><li><b>Troubleshoot network connectivity with Dynamic Verification (public preview)</b>&amp;#8212;You can now check packet loss rate and one-way network latency between two VMs on GCP. This capability is an addition to existing Network Intelligence Center Connectivity Tests which verify reachability by analyzing network configuration in your VPCs.&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/network-intelligence-center/docs/connectivity-tests&quot;>See more in our documentation.</a></li><li><b>Helping U.S. states get the COVID-19 vaccine to more people</b>&amp;#8212;In February, we announced our&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/public-sector/getting-vaccines-local-communities-safely-and-effectively&quot;>Intelligent Vaccine Impact solution (IVIs)</a>&amp;#160;to help communities rise to the challenge of getting vaccines to more people quickly and effectively. Many states have deployed IVIs, and have found it able to meet demand and easily integrate with their existing technology infrastructures. Google Cloud is proud to partner with a number of states across the U.S., including Arizona, the Commonwealth of Massachusetts, North Carolina, Oregon, and the Commonwealth of Virginia to support vaccination efforts at scale.&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/inside-google-cloud/how-google-cloud-is-supporting-covid-19-vaccination-efforts&quot;>Learn more</a>.</li></ul>">

The Google Cloud Tech YouTube channel has a series of whiteboard drawing board videos that explain cloud tools for technical practitioners in about 5 minutes each.</p>

                  <div _ngcontent-c19="" class="rich-text" innerhtml="<h3>Week of Mar 15-Mar 19 2021</h3><ul><li><b>A2 VMs now GA: The largest GPU cloud instances with NVIDIA A100 GPUs</b>&amp;#8212;We&amp;#8217;re announcing the general availability of A2 VMs based on the NVIDIA Ampere A100 Tensor Core GPUs in Compute Engine. This means customers around the world can now run their NVIDIA CUDA-enabled machine learning (ML) and high performance computing (HPC) scale-out and scale-up workloads more efficiently and at a lower cost.&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/compute/a2-vms-with-nvidia-a100-gpus-are-ga&quot;>Learn more</a>.<br></li><li><b>Earn the new Google Kubernetes Engine skill badge for free</b>&amp;#8212;We&amp;#8217;ve added a new <a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/training/badges&quot;>skill badge</a> this month, Optimize Costs for Google Kubernetes Engine (GKE), which you can earn for free when you sign up for the Kubernetes track of the <a href=&quot;https://inthecloud.withgoogle.com/google-cloud-skills/register.html?utm_source=google&amp;amp;utm_medium=blog&amp;amp;utm_campaign=FY21-Q1-global-trainingandenablement-website-other-skills_challenge&amp;amp;utm_content=gke_cost_optimization&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;>skills challenge</a>. The skills challenge provides 30 days free access to Google Cloud labs and gives you the opportunity to earn skill badges to showcase different cloud competencies to employers. <a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/training-certifications/how-to-get-the-new-optimize-costs-for-google-kubernetes-engine-skills-badge&quot;>Learn more</a>.<br></li><li><b>Now available: carbon free energy percentages for our Google Cloud regions</b>&amp;#8212;Google first achieved carbon neutrality in 2007, and since 2017 we&amp;#8217;ve purchased enough solar and wind energy to match 100% of our global electricity consumption. Now we&amp;#8217;re building on that progress to target <a href=&quot;https://blog.google/outreach-initiatives/sustainability/our-third-decade-climate-action-realizing-carbon-free-future/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;>a new sustainability goal</a>: running our business on carbon-free energy 24/7, everywhere, by 2030. Beginning this week, we&amp;#8217;re sharing data about how we are performing against that objective so our customers can select Google Cloud regions based on the carbon-free energy supplying them. <a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/sustainability/sharing-carbon-free-energy-percentage-for-google-cloud-regions&quot;>Learn more</a>.<br></li><li><b>Increasing bandwidth to C2 and N2 VMs</b>&amp;#8212;We announced the public preview of 100, 75, and 50 Gbps high-bandwidth network configurations for <a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/compute/docs/machine-types#n2_standard_machine_types&quot;>General Purpose N2</a> and <a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/compute/docs/machine-types#c2_machine_types&quot;>Compute Optimized C2</a> Compute Engine VM families as part of <a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/networking/google-cloud-networking-in-depth-how-andromeda-2-2-enables-high-throughput-vms&quot;>continuous efforts to optimize our Andromeda host networking stack</a>. This means we can now offer higher-bandwidth options on existing VM families when using the <a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/compute/docs/networking/using-gvnic&quot;>Google Virtual NIC (gVNIC)</a>. These VMs were previously limited to 32 Gbps. <a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/networking/increasing-bandwidth-to-c2-and-n2-vms&quot;>Learn more</a>.</li><li><p><b>New research on how COVID-19 changed the nature of IT</b>&amp;#8212;To learn more about the impact of COVID-19 and the resulting implications to IT, Google commissioned a study by IDG to better understand how organizations are shifting their priorities in the wake of the pandemic.&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/research/new-research-covid-19s-surprising-acceleration-of-it-digital-transformation&quot;>Learn more</a>&amp;#160;and&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://inthecloud.withgoogle.com/it-leaders-research-21/overview-dl-cd.html?utm_source=google&amp;amp;utm_medium=blog&amp;amp;utm_campaign=FY21-Q1-NORTHAM-demandgen-website-wd-gcp_gtm_reimagine_master&amp;amp;utm_content=homepage&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;>download the report</a>.</p></li><li><p><b>New in API security</b>&amp;#8212;Google Cloud Apigee API management platform's latest release,&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/apigee&quot;>Apigee X</a>, works with&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/armor&quot;>Cloud Armor</a>&amp;#160;to protect your APIs with advanced security technology including DDoS protection, geo-fencing, OAuth, and API keys. Learn more about our integrated security enhancements&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/api-management/api-security-with-apigee-and-google-cloud-armor&quot;>here</a>.</p></li><li><p><b>Troubleshoot errors more quickly with Cloud Logging</b>&amp;#8212;The Logs Explorer now automatically breaks down your log results by severity, making it easy to spot spikes in errors at specific times. Learn more about our new histogram functionality&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/logging/docs/view/logs-viewer-interface#histogram-panel&quot;>here</a>.</p></li></ul>">
                   <h3>Week of Mar 15-Mar 19 2021</h3>
                   <ul>
                    <li><b>A2 VMs now GA: The largest GPU cloud instances with NVIDIA A100 GPUs</b>Were announcing the general availability of A2 VMs based on the NVIDIA Ampere A100 Tensor Core GPUs in Compute Engine. This means customers around the world can now run their NVIDIA CUDA-enabled machine learning (ML) and high performance computing (HPC) scale-out and scale-up workloads more efficiently and at a lower cost.&nbsp;<a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/compute/a2-vms-with-nvidia-a100-gpus-are-ga" track-type="inline link" track-name="197" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/compute/a2-vms-with-nvidia-a100-gpus-are-ga" track-metadata-module="post">Learn more</a>.<br></li>
                    <li><b>Earn the new Google Kubernetes Engine skill badge for free</b>Weve added a new <a href="https://cloud.google.com/training/badges" track-type="inline link" track-name="198" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/training/badges" track-metadata-module="post">skill badge</a> this month, Optimize Costs for Google Kubernetes Engine (GKE), which you can earn for free when you sign up for the Kubernetes track of the <a href="https://inthecloud.withgoogle.com/google-cloud-skills/register.html?utm_source=google&amp;utm_medium=blog&amp;utm_campaign=FY21-Q1-global-trainingandenablement-website-other-skills_challenge&amp;utm_content=gke_cost_optimization" target="_blank" track-type="inline link" track-name="199" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://inthecloud.withgoogle.com" track-metadata-module="post">skills challenge</a>. The skills challenge provides 30 days free access to Google Cloud labs and gives you the opportunity to earn skill badges to showcase different cloud competencies to employers. <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/training-certifications/how-to-get-the-new-optimize-costs-for-google-kubernetes-engine-skills-badge" track-type="inline link" track-name="200" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/training-certifications/how-to-get-the-new-optimize-costs-for-google-kubernetes-engine-skills-badge" track-metadata-module="post">Learn more</a>.<br></li>
                    <li><b>Now available: carbon free energy percentages for our Google Cloud regions</b>Google first achieved carbon neutrality in 2007, and since 2017 weve purchased enough solar and wind energy to match 100% of our global electricity consumption. Now were building on that progress to target <a href="https://blog.google/outreach-initiatives/sustainability/our-third-decade-climate-action-realizing-carbon-free-future/" target="_blank" track-type="inline link" track-name="201" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://blog.google" track-metadata-module="post">a new sustainability goal</a>: running our business on carbon-free energy 24/7, everywhere, by 2030. Beginning this week, were sharing data about how we are performing against that objective so our customers can select Google Cloud regions based on the carbon-free energy supplying them. <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/sustainability/sharing-carbon-free-energy-percentage-for-google-cloud-regions" track-type="inline link" track-name="202" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/sustainability/sharing-carbon-free-energy-percentage-for-google-cloud-regions" track-metadata-module="post">Learn more</a>.<br></li>
                    <li><b>Increasing bandwidth to C2 and N2 VMs</b>We announced the public preview of 100, 75, and 50 Gbps high-bandwidth network configurations for <a href="https://cloud.google.com/compute/docs/machine-types#n2_standard_machine_types" track-type="inline link" track-name="203" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/compute/docs/machine-types#n2_standard_machine_types" track-metadata-module="post">General Purpose N2</a> and <a href="https://cloud.google.com/compute/docs/machine-types#c2_machine_types" track-type="inline link" track-name="204" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/compute/docs/machine-types#c2_machine_types" track-metadata-module="post">Compute Optimized C2</a> Compute Engine VM families as part of <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/networking/google-cloud-networking-in-depth-how-andromeda-2-2-enables-high-throughput-vms" track-type="inline link" track-name="205" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/networking/google-cloud-networking-in-depth-how-andromeda-2-2-enables-high-throughput-vms" track-metadata-module="post">continuous efforts to optimize our Andromeda host networking stack</a>. This means we can now offer higher-bandwidth options on existing VM families when using the <a href="https://cloud.google.com/compute/docs/networking/using-gvnic" track-type="inline link" track-name="206" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/compute/docs/networking/using-gvnic" track-metadata-module="post">Google Virtual NIC (gVNIC)</a>. These VMs were previously limited to 32 Gbps. <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/networking/increasing-bandwidth-to-c2-and-n2-vms" track-type="inline link" track-name="207" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/networking/increasing-bandwidth-to-c2-and-n2-vms" track-metadata-module="post">Learn more</a>.</li>
                    <li><p><b>New research on how COVID-19 changed the nature of IT</b>To learn more about the impact of COVID-19 and the resulting implications to IT, Google commissioned a study by IDG to better understand how organizations are shifting their priorities in the wake of the pandemic.&nbsp;<a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/research/new-research-covid-19s-surprising-acceleration-of-it-digital-transformation" track-type="inline link" track-name="208" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/research/new-research-covid-19s-surprising-acceleration-of-it-digital-transformation" track-metadata-module="post">Learn more</a>&nbsp;and&nbsp;<a href="https://inthecloud.withgoogle.com/it-leaders-research-21/overview-dl-cd.html?utm_source=google&amp;utm_medium=blog&amp;utm_campaign=FY21-Q1-NORTHAM-demandgen-website-wd-gcp_gtm_reimagine_master&amp;utm_content=homepage" target="_blank" track-type="inline link" track-name="209" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://inthecloud.withgoogle.com" track-metadata-module="post">download the report</a>.</p></li>
                    <li><p><b>New in API security</b>Google Cloud Apigee API management platform's latest release,&nbsp;<a href="https://cloud.google.com/apigee" track-type="inline link" track-name="210" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/apigee" track-metadata-module="post">Apigee X</a>, works with&nbsp;<a href="https://cloud.google.com/armor" track-type="inline link" track-name="211" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/armor" track-metadata-module="post">Cloud Armor</a>&nbsp;to protect your APIs with advanced security technology including DDoS protection, geo-fencing, OAuth, and API keys. Learn more about our integrated security enhancements&nbsp;<a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/api-management/api-security-with-apigee-and-google-cloud-armor" track-type="inline link" track-name="212" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/api-management/api-security-with-apigee-and-google-cloud-armor" track-metadata-module="post">here</a>.</p></li>
                    <li><p><b>Troubleshoot errors more quickly with Cloud Logging</b>The Logs Explorer now automatically breaks down your log results by severity, making it easy to spot spikes in errors at specific times. Learn more about our new histogram functionality&nbsp;<a href="https://cloud.google.com/logging/docs/view/logs-viewer-interface#histogram-panel" track-type="inline link" track-name="213" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/logging/docs/view/logs-viewer-interface#histogram-panel" track-metadata-module="post">here</a>.</p></li>
                   </ul>

                  <div _ngcontent-c19="" class="rich-text" innerhtml="<h3>Week of Mar 1-Mar 5 2021<br></h3><ul><li>Cloud Run&amp;#160;is now available in all Google Cloud regions.&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/run/docs/locations&quot;>Learn more</a>.<br></li><li>Introducing Apache Spark Structured Streaming connector for Pub/Sub Lite&amp;#8212;We&amp;#8217;re announcing the release of an open source&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://github.com/googleapis/java-pubsublite-spark&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;>connector</a>&amp;#160;to read streams of messages from&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/pubsub/lite/docs&quot;>Pub/Sub Lite</a>&amp;#160;into Apache Spark.The connector&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://github.com/googleapis/java-pubsublite-spark#downloading-and-using-the-connector&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;>works</a>&amp;#160;in all Apache Spark 2.4.X distributions, including Dataproc, Databricks, or manual Spark installations.&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/data-analytics/pubsub-lite-for-your-streaming-applications&quot;>Learn more</a>.<br></li><li>Google Cloud Next &amp;#8216;21 is October 12-14, 2021&amp;#8212;Join us and learn how the most successful companies have transformed their businesses with Google Cloud. Sign-up at&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.withgoogle.com/next/sf?utm_source=google&amp;amp;utm_medium=blog&amp;amp;utm_campaign=FY21-Q1-Google-Cloud-Blog&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;>g.co/cloudnext</a>&amp;#160;for updates.&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/google-cloud-next/announcing-google-cloud-next21&quot;>Learn more</a>.<br></li><li>Hierarchical firewall policies now GA&amp;#8212;Hierarchical firewalls provide a means to enforce firewall rules at the&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/resource-manager/docs/creating-managing-organization&quot;>organization</a>&amp;#160;and&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/resource-manager/docs/creating-managing-folders&quot;>folder</a>&amp;#160;levels in the&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/resource-manager/docs/cloud-platform-resource-hierarchy&quot;>GCP Resource Hierarchy</a>. This allows security administrators at different levels in the hierarchy to define and deploy consistent firewall rules across a number of projects so they're applied to all VMs in currently existing and yet-to-be-created projects.&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/new-google-cloud-hierarchical-firewall-policies&quot;>Learn more</a>.<br></li><li>Announcing the Google Cloud Born-Digital Summit&amp;#8212;Over this half-day event, we&amp;#8217;ll highlight proven best-practice approaches to data, architecture, diversity &amp;amp;                   <div _ngcontent-c19="" class="rich-text" innerhtml="<h3>Week of Feb 22-Feb 26 2021</h3><ul><li><p>21 Google Cloud tools explained in 2 minutes&amp;#8212;Need a quick overview of Google Cloud core technologies? Quickly learn these 21 Google Cloud products&amp;#8212;each explained in under two minutes.&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/inside-google-cloud/21-google-cloud-tools-each-explained-under-2-minutes&quot;>Learn more</a>.</p></li><li><p>BigQuery materialized views now GA&amp;#8212;Materialized views (MV&amp;#8217;s) are precomputed views that periodically cache results of a query to provide customers increased performance and efficiency.&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/data-analytics/bigquery-materialized-views-now-ga&quot;>Learn more</a>.</p></li><li><p>New in BigQuery BI Engine&amp;#8212;We&amp;#8217;re extending BigQuery BI Engine to work with any BI or custom dashboarding applications that require sub-second query response times. In this preview, BI Engine will work seamlessly with Looker and other popular BI tools such as Tableau and Power BI without requiring any change to the BI tools.&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/data-analytics/bigquery-bi-engine-extends-integration-for-any-bi-solution&quot;>Learn more</a>.</p></li><li><p>Dataproc now supports Shielded VMs&amp;#8212;All Dataproc clusters created using Debian 10 or Ubuntu 18.04 operating systems now use&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/security/shielded-cloud/shielded-vm&quot;>Shielded VMs</a>&amp;#160;by default and customers can provide their own&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/dataproc/docs/reference/rest/v1/ClusterConfig#ShieldedInstanceConfig&quot;>configurations</a>&amp;#160;for secure boot, vTPM, and Integrity Monitoring. This feature is just one of the many ways customers that have migrated their Hadoop and Spark clusters to GCP experience continued improvements to their security postures without any additional cost.<br></p></li><li><p>New Cloud Security Podcast by Google&amp;#8212;Our new podcast brings you stories and insights on security in the cloud, delivering security from the cloud, and, of course, on what we&amp;#8217;re doing at Google Cloud to help keep customer data safe and workloads secure.&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/introducing-google-clouds-new-cloud-security-podcast&quot;>Learn more</a>.<br></p></li><li><p>New in Conversational AI and Apigee technology&amp;#8212;Australian retailer Woolworths provides seamless customer experiences with their virtual agent, Olive. Apigee API Management and Dialogflow technology allows customers to talk to Olive through voice and chat.&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/api-management/conversational-ai-with-dialogflow-and-apigee-api-management&quot;>Learn more</a>.<br></p></li><li><p>Introducing GKE Autopilot&amp;#8212;GKE already offers an industry-leading level of automation that makes setting up and operating a Kubernetes cluster easier and more cost effective than do-it-yourself and other managed offerings. Autopilot represents a significant leap forward. In addition to the fully managed control plane that GKE has always provided, using the Autopilot mode of operation automatically applies industry best practices and can eliminate all node management operations, maximizing your cluster efficiency and helping to provide a stronger security posture.&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/containers-kubernetes/introducing-gke-autopilot&quot;>Learn more</a>.<br></p></li><li><p>Partnering with Intel to accelerate cloud-native 5G&amp;#8212;As we continue to grow cloud-native services for the telecommunications industry, we&amp;#8217;re excited to announce a collaboration with Intel to develop reference architectures and integrated solutions for communications service providers to accelerate their deployment of 5G and edge network solutions.&amp;#160;<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/partners/speeding-up-cloud-native-5g-networks-with-intel-and-google-cloud&quot;>Learn more</a>.</p></li><li><p>Veeam Backup for Google Cloud now available&amp;#8212;<a href=&quot;https://www.veeam.com/blog/google-cloud-backup-and-recovery.html&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;>Veeam Backup for Google Cloud</a>&amp;#160;automates Google-native snapshots to securely protect VMs across projects and regions with ultra-low RPOs and RTOs, and store backups in Google Object Storage to enhance data protection while ensuring lower costs for long-term retention.</p></li><li><p>Migrate for Anthos 1.6 GA&amp;#8212;With<a href=&quot;https://cloud.google.com/migrate/anthos/docs&quot;>&amp;#160;Migrate for Anthos</a>, customers and partners can automatically migrate and modernize traditional application workloads running in VMs into containers running on Anthos or GKE. Included in this new release:&amp;#160;</p></li><ul><li><p>In-place modernization for Anthos on AWS (Public Preview) to help customers accelerate on-boarding to Anthos AWS while leveraging their existing investment in AWS data sources, projects, VPCs, and IAM controls.</p></li><li><p>Additional Docker registries and artifacts repositories support (GA) including AWS ECR, basic-auth docker registries, and AWS S3 storage to provide further flexibility for customers using Anthos Anywhere (on-prem, AWS, etc).&amp;#160;</p></li><li><p>HTTPS Proxy support (GA) to enable M4A functionality (access to external image repos and other services) where a proxy is used to control external access.</p></li></ul></ul>">

                    <li><p>New Cloud Security Podcast by GoogleOur new podcast brings you stories and insights on security in the cloud, delivering security from the cloud, and, of course, on what were doing at Google Cloud to help keep customer data safe and workloads secure.&nbsp;<a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/introducing-google-clouds-new-cloud-security-podcast" track-type="inline link" track-name="245" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/introducing-google-clouds-new-cloud-security-podcast" track-metadata-module="post">Learn more</a>.<br></p></li>

                    <li><p>Migrate for Anthos 1.6 GAWith<a href="https://cloud.google.com/migrate/anthos/docs" track-type="inline link" track-name="250" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/migrate/anthos/docs" track-metadata-module="post">&nbsp;Migrate for Anthos</a>, customers and partners can automatically migrate and modernize traditional application workloads running in VMs into containers running on Anthos or GKE. Included in this new release:&nbsp;</p></li>
                    <ul>
                     <li><p>In-place modernization for Anthos on AWS (Public Preview) to help customers accelerate on-boarding to Anthos AWS while leveraging their existing investment in AWS data sources, projects, VPCs, and IAM controls.</p></li>

                   <ul>
                    <li><p>Introducing Cloud Domains in previewCloud Domains simplify domain registration and management within Google Cloud, improve the custom domain experience for developers, increase security, and support stronger integrations around DNS and SSL.&nbsp;<a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/networking/introducing-cloud-domains" track-type="inline link" track-name="251" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/networking/introducing-cloud-domains" track-metadata-module="post">Learn more</a>.</p></li>
