                   <ul>
                    <li><p><b>New, lower pricing for Cloud CDN</b>Weve reduced the price of cache fill (content fetched from your origin) charges across the board, by up to 80%, along with our recent introduction of <a href="https://cloud.google.com/cdn/docs/release-notes#September_14_2020" track-type="inline link" track-name="352" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/cdn/docs/release-notes#September_14_2020" track-metadata-module="post">a new set of flexible caching capabilities</a>, to make it even easier to use Cloud CDN to optimize the performance of your applications. <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/networking/introducing-lower-simpler-pricing-for-cloud-cdn" track-type="inline link" track-name="353" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/networking/introducing-lower-simpler-pricing-for-cloud-cdn" track-metadata-module="post">Read the blog</a>.<br></p></li>
                    <li><p><b>Expanding the BeyondCorp Alliance</b>Last year, we announced our BeyondCorp Alliance with partners that share our Zero Trust vision. Today, were announcing new partners to this alliance. <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/google-cloud-announces-new-partners-in-its-beyondcorp-alliance" track-type="inline link" track-name="354" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/google-cloud-announces-new-partners-in-its-beyondcorp-alliance" track-metadata-module="post">Read the blog</a>.</p></li>
                    <li><p><b>New data analytics training opportunities</b>Throughout October and November, were offering a number of no-cost ways to learn data analytics, with trainings for beginners to advanced users. <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/training-certifications/google-cloud-data-analytics-training-for-all-skills-levels" track-type="inline link" track-name="355" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/training-certifications/google-cloud-data-analytics-training-for-all-skills-levels" track-metadata-module="post">Learn more</a>.</p></li>
                    <li><p><b>New BigQuery blog series</b>BigQuery Explained provides overviews on storage, data ingestion, queries, joins, and more. <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/developers-practitioners/bigquery-explained-blog-series" track-type="inline link" track-name="356" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/developers-practitioners/bigquery-explained-blog-series" track-metadata-module="post">Read the series</a>.</p></li>
                   </ul>
                   <h3>
                    <hr></h3>
                   <h3>Week of Oct 5-9 2020</h3>
                   <ul>
                    <li><p><b>Introducing the Google Cloud Healthcare Consent Management API</b>This API gives healthcare application developers and clinical researchers a simple way to manage individuals consent of their health data, particularly important given the new and emerging virtual care and research scenarios related to COVID-19. <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/healthcare-life-sciences/googles-healthcare-consent-management-api-protects-user-data" track-type="inline link" track-name="357" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/healthcare-life-sciences/googles-healthcare-consent-management-api-protects-user-data" track-metadata-module="post">Read the blog</a>.</p></li>
                    <li><p><b>Announcing Google Cloud buildpacks</b>Based on the CNCF buildpacks v3 specification, these buildpacks produce container images that follow best practices and are suitable for running on all of our container platforms: Cloud Run (fully managed), Anthos, and Google Kubernetes Engine (GKE). <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/containers-kubernetes/google-cloud-now-supports-buildpacks" track-type="inline link" track-name="358" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/containers-kubernetes/google-cloud-now-supports-buildpacks" track-metadata-module="post">Read the blog</a>.</p></li>
                    <li><p><b>Providing open access to the Genome Aggregation Database (gnomAD)</b>Our collaboration with Broad Institute of MIT and Harvard provides free access to one of the world's most comprehensive public genomic datasets. <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/healthcare-life-sciences/google-cloud-providing-free-access-to-genome-aggregation-database" track-type="inline link" track-name="359" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/healthcare-life-sciences/google-cloud-providing-free-access-to-genome-aggregation-database" track-metadata-module="post">Read the blog</a>.</p></li>
                    <li><p><b>Introducing HTTP/gRPC server streaming for Cloud Run</b>Server-side HTTP streaming for your serverless applications running on Cloud Run (fully managed) is now available. This means your Cloud Run services can serve larger responses or stream partial responses to clients during the span of a single request, enabling quicker server response times for your applications. <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/serverless/cloud-run-now-supports-http-grpc-server-streaming" track-type="inline link" track-name="360" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/serverless/cloud-run-now-supports-http-grpc-server-streaming" track-metadata-module="post">Read the blog</a>.</p></li>
                    <li><p><b>New security and privacy features in Google Workspace</b>Alongside the announcement of Google Workspace we also shared more information on new security features that help facilitate safe communication and give admins increased visibility and control for their organizations. <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/workspace/announcing-new-security-and-privacy-updates-in-google-workspace" track-type="inline link" track-name="361" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/workspace/announcing-new-security-and-privacy-updates-in-google-workspace" track-metadata-module="post">Read the blog</a>.</p></li>
                    <li><p><b>Introducing Google Workspace</b>Google Workspace includes all of the productivity apps you know and use at home, at work, or in the classroomGmail, Calendar, Drive, Docs, Sheets, Slides, Meet, Chat and morenow more thoughtfully connected. <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/workspace/introducing-google-workspace" track-type="inline link" track-name="362" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/workspace/introducing-google-workspace" track-metadata-module="post">Read the blog</a>.</p></li>
                    <li><p><b>New in Cloud Functions: languages, availability, portability, and more</b>We extended Cloud Functionsour scalable pay-as-you-go Functions-as-a-Service (FaaS) platform that runs your code with zero server managementso you can now use it to build end-to-end solutions for several key use cases. <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/serverless/a-roundup-of-cloud-functions-enhancements" track-type="inline link" track-name="363" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/serverless/a-roundup-of-cloud-functions-enhancements" track-metadata-module="post">Read the blog</a>.</p></li>
                    <li><p><b>Announcing the Google Cloud Public Sector Summit, Dec 8-9</b>Our upcoming two-day virtual event will offer thought-provoking panels, keynotes, customer stories and more on the future of digital service in the public sector. <a href="https://cloudonair.withgoogle.com/events/public-sector-summit?utm_source=google&amp;utm_medium=blog&amp;utm_campaign=-&amp;utm_content=google-living-blog" target="_blank" track-type="inline link" track-name="364" track-metadata-eventdetail="https://cloudonair.withgoogle.com" track-metadata-module="post">Register at no cost</a>.</p></li>
                   </ul>

target=\&q;_blank\&q;&g;whitepaper&l;/a&g;.&l;br/&g;&l;/li&g;&l;li&g;&l;b&g;Active Assists new feature,&l;i&g;predictive autoscaling&l;/i&g;, helps improve response times for your applications&l;/b&g;When you enable predictive autoscaling, Compute Engine forecasts future load based on your Managed Instance Groups (MIG) history and scales it out in advance of predicted load, so that new instances are ready to serve when the load arrives. Without predictive autoscaling, an autoscaler can only scale a group reactively, based on observed changes in load in real time. With predictive autoscaling enabled, the autoscaler works with real-time data as well as with historical data to cover both the current and forecasted load. That makes predictive autoscaling ideal for those apps with long initialization times and whose workloads vary predictably with daily or weekly cycles. For more information, see&l;a href=\&q;https://cloud.google.com/compute/docs/autoscaler/predictive-autoscaling#how_predictive_autoscaling_works\&q;&g;How predictive autoscaling works&l;/a&g;or&l;a href=\&q;https://cloud.google.com/compute/docs/autoscaler/predictive-autoscaling#checking_if_predictive_autoscaling_is_suitable_for_your_workload\&q;&g;check if predictive autoscaling is suitable for your workload&l;/a&g;, and to learn more about other intelligent features, check out&l;a href=\&q;https://cloud.google.com/solutions/active-assist\&q;&g;Active Assist&l;/a&g;.&l;br/&g;&l;/li&g;&l;li&g;&l;b&g;Introducing Dataprep BigQuery pushdown&l;/b&g;BigQuery pushdown gives you the flexibility to run jobs using either BigQuery or Dataflow. If you select BigQuery, then Dataprep can automatically determine if data pipelines can be partially or fully translated in a BigQuery SQL statement. Any portions of the pipeline that cannot be run in BigQuery are executed in Dataflow. Utilizing the power of BigQuery results in highly efficient data transformations, especially for manipulations such as filters, joins, unions, and aggregations. This leads to better performance, optimized costs, and increased security with IAM and OAuth support.&l;a href=\&q;https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/data-analytics/introducing-dataprep-bigquery-pushdown\&q;&g;Learn more&l;/a&g;.&l;br/&g;&l;/li&g;&l;li&g;&l;b&g;Announcing the Google Cloud Retail &a;amp; Consumer Goods Summit&l;/b&g;The Google Cloud Retail &a;amp; Consumer Goods Summit brings together technology and business insights, the key ingredients for any transformation. Autopilot represents a significant leap forward.
